trīṇi mahāmunec taptvā suduṣkaraṃ prāpto brahmalokam anuttamama tato māṃ svargasaṃsthaṃ vai kṣutpipāse dvijottamac bādhete paramodāra tato haṃ vyathitendriyaḥa gatvā tribhuvaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ pitāmaham uvāca hac bhagavan brahmaloko yaṃ kṣutpipāsāvivarjitaḥa kasyeyaṃ karmaṇaḥ prāptiḥ kṣutpipāsāvaśo smi yatc āhāraḥ kaś ca me deva tan me brūhi pitāmahaa pitāmahas tu mām āha tavāhāraḥ sudevajac svādūni svāni māṃsāni tāni bhakṣaya nityaśaḥa svaśarīraṃ tvayā puṣṭaṃ kurvatā tapa uttamamc anuptaṃ rohate śveta na kadā cin mahāmatea dattaṃ na te sti sūkṣmo pi vane sattvaniṣevitec tena svargagato vatsa bādhyase kṣutpipāsayāa sa tvaṃ supuṣṭam āhāraiḥ svaśarīram anuttamamc bhakṣayasvāmṛtarasaṃ sā te tṛptir bhaviṣyatia yadā tu tad vanaṃ śveta agastyaḥ sumahān ṛṣiḥc ākramiṣyati durdharṣas tadā kṛcchād vimokṣyasea sa hi tārayituṃ saumya śaktaḥ suragaṇān apic kiṃ punas tvāṃ mahābāho kṣutpipāsāvaśaṃ gatama so haṃ bhagavataḥ śrutvā devadevasya niścayamc āhāraṃ garhitaṃ kurmi svaśarīraṃ dvijottamaa bahūn varṣagaṇān brahman bhujyamānam idaṃ mayāc kṣayaṃ nābhyeti brahmarṣe tṛptiś cāpi mamottamāa tasya me kṛcchrabhūtasya kṛcchrād asmād vimokṣayac anyeṣām agatir hy atra kumbhayonim ṛte dvijama idam ābharaṇaṃ saumya tāraṇārthaṃ dvijottamac pratigṛhṇīṣva brahmarṣe prasādaṃ kartum arhasia tasyāhaṃ svargiṇo vākyaṃ śrutvā duḥkhasamanvitamc tāraṇāyopajagrāha tad ābharaṇam uttamama mayā pratigṛhīte tu tasminn ābharaṇe śubhec mānuṣaḥ pūrvako deho rājarṣeḥ sa nanāśa haa pranaṣṭe tu śarīre sau rājarṣiḥ parayā mudāc tṛptaḥ pramudito rājā jagāma tridivaṃ punaḥa tenedaṃ śakratulyena divyam ābharaṇaṃ mamac tasmin nimitte kākutstha dattam adbhutadarśanama tad adbhutatamaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvāgastyasya rāghavaḥc gauravād vismayāc caiva bhūyaḥ praṣṭuṃ pracakramea bhagavaṃs tad vanaṃ ghoraṃ tapas tapyati yatra saḥc śveto vaidarbhako rājā kathaṃ tad amṛgadvijama niḥsattvaṃ ca vanaṃ jātaṃ śūnyaṃ manujavarjitamc tapaś cartuṃ praviṣṭaḥ sa śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥa rāmasya bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā kautūhalasamanvitamc vākyaṃ paramatejasvī vaktum evopacakramea purā kṛtayuge rāma manur daṇḍadharaḥ prabhuḥc tasya putro mahān āsīd ikṣvākuḥ kulavardhanaḥa taṃ putraṃ pūrvake rājye nikṣipya bhuvi durjayamc pṛthivyāṃ rājavaṃśānāṃ bhava kartety uvāca haa tatheti ca pratijñātaṃ pituḥ putreṇa rāghavac tataḥ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo manuḥ punar uvāca haa prīto smi paramodārakartā cāsi na saṃśayaḥc daṇḍena ca prajā rakṣa mā ca daṇḍam akāraṇea aparādhiṣu yo daṇḍaḥ pātyate mānaveṣu vaic sa daṇḍo vidhivan muktaḥ svargaṃ nayati pārthivama tasmād daṇḍe mahābāho yatnavān bhava putrakac dharmo hi paramo loke kurvatas te bhaviṣyatia iti taṃ bahu saṃdiśya manuḥ putraṃ samādhināc jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭo brahmalokam anuttamama prayāte tridive tasminn ikṣvākur amitaprabhaḥc janayiṣye kathaṃ putrān iti cintāparo bhavata karmabhir bahurūpaiś ca tais tair manusutaḥ sutānc janayām āsa dharmātmā śataṃ devasutopamāna teṣām avarajas tāta sarveṣāṃ raghunandanac mūḍhaś cākṛtividyaś ca na śuśrūṣati pūrvajāna nāma tasya ca daṇḍeti pitā cakre lpatejasaḥc avaśyaṃ daṇḍapatanaṃ śarīre sya bhaviṣyatia sa paśyamānas taṃ doṣaṃ ghoraṃ putrasya rāghavac vindhyaśaivalayor madhye rājyaṃ prādād ariṃdamaa sa daṇḍas tatra rājābhūd ramye parvatarodhasic puraṃ cāpratimaṃ rāma nyaveśayad anuttamama purasya cākaron nāma madhumantam iti prabhoc purohitaṃ cośanasaṃ varayām āsa suvratama evaṃ sa rājā tad rājyaṃ kārayat sapurohitaḥc prahṛṣṭamanujākīrṇaṃ devarājyaṃ yathā divia etad ākhyāya rāmāya maharṣiḥ kumbhasaṃbhavaḥc asyām evāparaṃ vākyaṃ kathāyām upacakramea tataḥ sa daṇḍaḥ kākutstha bahuvarṣagaṇāyutamc akarot tatra mandātmā rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakama atha kāle tu kasmiṃś cid rājā bhārgavam āśramamc ramaṇīyam upākrāmac caitre māsi manoramea tatra bhārgavakanyāṃ sa rūpeṇāpratimāṃ bhuvic vicarantīṃ vanoddeśe daṇḍo paśyad anuttamāma sa dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sudurmedhā anaṅgaśarapīḍitaḥc abhigamya susaṃvignaḥ kanyāṃ vacanam abravīta kutas tvam asi suśroṇi kasya vāsi sutā śubhec pīḍito ham anaṅgena pṛcchāmi tvāṃ sumadhyamea tasya tv evaṃ bruvāṇasya mohonmattasya kāminaḥc bhārgavī pratyuvācedaṃ vacaḥ sānunayaṃ nṛpama bhārgavasya sutāṃ viddhi devasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥc arajāṃ nāma rājendra jyeṣṭhām āśramavāsinīma guruḥ pitā me rājendra tvaṃ ca śiṣyo mahātmanaḥc vyasanaṃ sumahat kruddhaḥ sa te dadyān mahātapāḥa yadi vātra mayā kāryaṃ dharmadṛṣṭena satpathāc varayasva nṛpa śreṣṭha pitaraṃ me mahādyutima anyathā tu phalaṃ tubhyaṃ bhaved ghorābhisaṃhitamc krodhena hi pitā me sau trailokyam api nirdaheta evaṃ bruvāṇām arajāṃ daṇḍaḥ kāmaśarārditaḥc pratyuvāca madonmattaḥ śirasy ādhāya so ñjalima prasādaṃ kuru suśroṇi na kālaṃ kṣeptum arhasic tvatkṛte hi mama prāṇā vidīryante śubhānanea tvāṃ prāpya hi vadho vāpi pāpaṃ vāpi sudāruṇamc bhaktaṃ bhajasva māṃ bhīru bhajamānaṃ suvihvalama evam uktvā tu tāṃ kanyāṃ dorbhyāṃ gṛhya balād balīc visphurantīṃ yathākāmaṃ maithunāyopacakramea tam anarthaṃ mahāghoraṃ daṇḍaḥ kṛtvā sudāruṇamc nagaraṃ prayayau cāśu madhumantam anuttamama arajāpi rudantī sā āśramasyāvidūrataḥc pratīkṣate susaṃtrastā pitaraṃ devasaṃnibhama sa muhūrtād upaśrutya devarṣir amitaprabhaḥc svam āśramaṃ śiṣya vṛtaḥ kṣudhārtaḥ saṃnyavartataa so paśyad arajāṃ dīnāṃ rajasā samabhiplutāmc jyotsnām ivāruṇagrastāṃ pratyūṣe na virājatīma tasya roṣaḥ samabhavat kṣudhārtasya viśeṣataḥc nirdahann iva lokāṃs trīñ śiṣyāṃś cedam uvāca haa paśyadhvaṃ viparītasya daṇḍasyāviditātmanaḥc vipattiṃ ghorasaṃkāśāṃ kruddhām agniśikhām ivaa kṣayo sya durmateḥ prāptaḥ sānugasya durātmanaḥc yaḥ pradīptāṃ hutāśasya śikhāṃ vai spraṣṭum icchatia yasmāt sa kṛtavān pāpam īdṛśaṃ ghoradarśanamc tasmāt prāpsyati durmedhāḥ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥa saptarātreṇa rājāsau sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥc pāpakarmasamācāro vadhaṃ prāpsyati durmatiḥa samantād yojanaśataṃ viṣayaṃ cāsya durmateḥc dhakṣyate pāṃsuvarṣeṇa mahatā pākaśāsanaḥa sarvasattvāni yānīha sthāvarāṇi carāṇi cac mahatā pāṃsuvarṣeṇa nāśaṃ yāsyanti sarvaśaḥa daṇḍasya viṣayo yāvat tāvat sarvasamucchrayaḥc pāṃsubhuta ivālakṣyaḥ saptarātrād bhaviṣyatia ity uktvā krodhasaṃtapas tam āśramanivāsinamc janaṃ janapadānteṣu sthīyatām iti cābravīta śrutvā tūśasano vākyaṃ sa āśramāvasatho janaḥc niṣkrānto viṣayāt tasya sthānaṃ cakre tha bāhyataḥa sa tathoktvā munijanam arajām idam abravītc ihaiva vasa durmedhe āśrame susamāhitāa idaṃ yojanaparyantaṃ saraḥ suruciraprabhamc araje vijvarā bhuṅkṣva kālaś cātra pratīkṣyatāma tvatsamīpe tu ye sattvā vāsam eṣyanti tāṃ niśāmc avadhyāḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa te bhaviṣyanti nityadāa ity uktvā bhārgavo vāsam anyatra samupākramatc saptāhād bhasmasādbhūtaṃ yathoktaṃ brahmavādināa tasyāsau daṇḍaviṣayo vindhyaśaivalasānuṣuc śapto brahmarṣiṇā tena purā vaidharmake kṛtea tataḥ prabhṛti kākutstha daṇḍakāraṇyam ucyatec tapasvinaḥ sthitā yatra janasthānam atho bhavata etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ pṛcchasi rāghavac saṃdhyām upāsituṃ vīra samayo hy ativartatea ete maharṣayaḥ sarve pūrṇakumbhāḥ samantataḥc kṛtodako naravyāghra ādityaṃ paryupāsatea sa tair ṛṣibhir abhyastaḥ sahitair brahmasattamaiḥc ravir astaṃ gato rāma gacchodakam upaspṛśaa ṛṣer vacanam ājñāya rāmaḥ saṃdhyām upāsitumc upākrāmat saraḥ puṇyam apsarobhir niṣevitama tatrodakam upaspṛṣśya saṃdhyām anvāsya paścimāmc āśramaṃ prāviśad rāmaḥ kumbhayoner mahātmanaḥa asyāgastyo bahuguṇaṃ phalamūlaṃ tathauṣadhīḥc śākāni ca pavitrāṇi bhojanārtham akalpayata sa bhuktavān naraśreṣṭhas tad annam amṛtopamamc prītaś ca parituṣṭaś ca tāṃ rātriṃ samupāvasata prabhāte kālyam utthāya kṛtvāhnikam ariṃdamaḥc ṛṣiṃ samabhicakrāma gamanāya raghūttamaḥa abhivādyābravīd rāmo maharṣiṃ kumbhasaṃbhavamc āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi mām anujñātum arhasia dhanyo smy anugṛhīto smi darśanena mahātmanaḥc draṣṭuṃ caivāgamiṣyāmi pāvanārtham ihātmanaḥa tathā vadati kākutsthe vākyam adbhutadarśanamc uvāca paramaprīto dharmanetras tapodhanaḥa atyadbhutam idaṃ vākyaṃ tava rāma śubhākṣaramc pāvanaḥ sarvalokānāṃ tvam eva raghunandanaa muhūrtam api rāma tvāṃ ye nu paśyanti ke canac pāvitāḥ svargabhūtās te pūjyante divi daivataiḥa ye ca tvāṃ ghoracakṣurbhir īkṣante prāṇino bhuvic hatās te yamadaṇḍena sadyo nirayagāminaḥa gaccha cāriṣṭam avyagraḥ panthānam akutobhayamc praśādhi rājyaṃ dharmeṇa gatir hi jagato bhavāna evam uktas tu muninā prāñjaliḥ prpagraho nṛpaḥc abhyavādayata prājñas tam ṛṣiṃ puṇyaśīlinama abhivādya muniśreṣṭhaṃ tāṃś ca sarvāṃs tapodhanānc adhyārohat tad avyagraḥ puṣpakaṃ hemabhūṣitama taṃ prayāntaṃ munigaṇā āśīrvādaiḥ samantataḥc apūjayan mahendrābhaṃ sahasrākṣam ivāmarāḥa svasthaḥ sa dadṛśe rāmaḥ puṣpake hemabhūṣitec śaśī meghasamīpastho yathā jaladharāgamea tato rdhadivase prāpte pūjyamānas tatas tataḥc ayodhyāṃ prāpya kākutstho vimānād avarohataa tato visṛjya ruciraṃ puṣpakaṃ kāmagāminamc kakṣyāntaravinikṣiptaṃ dvāḥsthaṃ rāmo bravīd vacaḥa lakṣmaṇaṃ bharataṃ caiva gatvā tau laghuvikramauc mamāgamanam ākhyāya śabdāpaya ca māṃ cirama tac chrutvā bhāṣitaṃ tasya rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥc dvāḥsthaḥ kumārāv āhūya rāghavāya nyavedayata dṛṣṭvā tu rāghavaḥ prāptau priyau bharatalakṣmaṇauc pariṣvajya tato rāmo vākyam etad uvāca haa kṛtaṃ mayā yathātathyaṃ dvijakāryam anuttamamc dharmasetumato bhūyaḥ kartum icchāmi rāghavaua yuvābhyām ātmabhūtābhyāṃ rājasūyam anuttamamc sahito yaṣṭum icchāmi tatra dharmo hi śāśvataḥa iṣṭvā tu rājasūyena mitraḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥc suhutena suyajñena varuṇatvam upāgamata somaś ca rājasūyena iṣṭvā dharmeṇa dharmavitc prāptaś ca sarvalokānāṃ kīrtiṃ sthānaṃ ca śāśvatama asminn ahani yac chreyaś cintyatāṃ tan mayā sahac hitaṃ cāyati yuktaṃ ca prayatau vaktum arhathaa śrutā tu rāghavasyaitad vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥc bharataḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā vākyam etad uvāca haa tvayi dharmaḥ paraḥ sādho tvayi sarvā vasuṃdharāc pratiṣṭhitā mahābāho yaśaś cāmitavikramaa mahīpālāś ca sarve tvāṃ prajāpatim ivāmarāḥc nirīkṣante mahātmāno lokanāthaṃ yathā vayama prajāś ca pitṛvad rājan paśyanti tvāṃ mahābalac pṛthivyāṃ gatibhūto si prāṇinām api rāghavaa sa tvam evaṃvidhaṃ yajñam āhartāsi kathaṃ nṛpac pṛthivyāṃ rājavaṃśānāṃ vināśo yatra dṛśyatea pṛthivyāṃ ye ca puruṣā rājan pauruṣam āgatāḥc sarveṣāṃ bhavitā tatra kṣayaḥ sarvāntakopamaḥa sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla guṇair atulavikramac pṛthivīṃ nārhase hantuṃ vaśe hi tava vartatea bharatasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvāmṛtamayaṃ yathāc praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥa uvāca ca śubhāṃ vāṇīṃ kaikeyyā nandivardhanamc prīto smi parituṣṭo smi tavādya vacanena hia idaṃ vacanam aklībaṃ tvayā dharmasamāhitamc vyāhṛtaṃ puruṣavyāghra pṛthivyāḥ paripālanama eṣa tasmād abhiprāyād rājasūyāt kratūttamānc nivartayāmi dharmajña tava suvyāhṛtena vaia prajānāṃ pālanaṃ dharmo rājñāṃ yajñena saṃmitaḥc tasmāc chṛṇomi te vākyaṃ sādhūktaṃ susamāhitama tathoktavati rāme tu bharate ca mahātmanic lakṣmaṇo pi śubhaṃ vākyam uvāca raghunandanama aśvamedho mahāyajñaḥ pāvanaḥ sarvapāpmanāmc pāvanas tava durdharṣo rocatāṃ kratupuṃgavaḥa śrūyate hi purāvṛttaṃ vāsave sumahātmanic brahmahatyāvṛtaḥ śakro hayamedhena pāvitaḥa purā kila mahābāho devāsurasamāgamec vṛtro nāma mahān āsīd daiteyo lokasaṃmataḥa vistīrṇā yojanaśatam ucchritas triguṇaṃ tataḥc anurāgeṇa lokāṃs trīn snehāt paśyati sarvataḥa dharmajñaś ca kṛtajñaś ca buddhyā ca pariniṣṭhitaḥc śaśāsa pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ dharmeṇa susamāhitaḥa tasmin praśāsati tadā sarvakāmadughā mahīc rasavanti prasūtāni mūlāni ca phalāni caa akṛṣṭapacyā pṛthivī susaṃpannā mahātmanaḥc sa rājyaṃ tādṛśaṃ bhuṅkte sphītam adbhutadarśanama tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā tapaḥ kuryām anuttamamc tapo hi paramaṃ śreyas tapo hi paramaṃ sukhama sa nikṣipya sutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ paureṣu parameśvaramc tapa ugram upātiṣṭhat tāpayan sarvadevatāḥa tapas tapyati vṛtre tu vāsavaḥ paramārtavatc viṣṇuṃ samupasaṃkramya vākyam etad uvāca haa tapasyatā mahābāho lokā vṛtreṇa nirjitāḥc balavān sa hi dharmātmā nainaṃ śakṣyāmi bādhituma yady asau tapa ātiṣṭhed bhūya eva sureśvarac yāval lokā dhariṣyanti tāvad asya vaśānugāḥa tvaṃ cainaṃ paramodāram upekṣasi mahābalac kṣaṇaṃ hi na bhaved vṛtraḥ kruddhe tvayi sureśvaraa yadā hi prītisaṃyogaṃ tvayā viṣṇo samāgataḥc tadā prabhṛti lokānāṃ nāthatvam upalabdhavāna sa tvaṃ prasādaṃ lokānāṃ kuruṣva sumahāyaśaḥc tvatkṛtena hi sarvaṃ syāt praśāntam ajaraṃ jagata ime hi sarve viṣṇo tvāṃ nirīkṣante divaukasaḥc vṛtraghatena mahatā eṣāṃ sāhyaṃ kuruṣva haa tvayā hi nityaśaḥ sāhyaṃ kṛtam eṣāṃ mahātmanāmc asahyam idam anyeṣām agatīnāṃ gatir bhavāna lakṣmaṇasya tu tad vākyaṃ śrutvā śatrunibarhaṇaḥc vṛtraghātam aśeṣeṇa kathayety āha lakṣmaṇama rāghaveṇaivam uktas tu sumitrānandavardhanaḥc bhūya eva kathāṃ divyāṃ kathayām āsa lakṣmaṇaḥa sahasrākṣavacaḥ śrutvā sarveṣāṃ ca divaukasāmc viṣṇur devān uvācedaṃ sarvān indrapurogamāna pūrvaṃ sauhṛdabaddho smi vṛtrasya sumahātmanaḥc tena yuṣmat priyārthaṃ vai nāhaṃ hanmi mahāsurama avaśyaṃ karaṇīyaṃ ca bhavatāṃ sukham uttamamc tasmād upāyam ākhyāsye yena vṛtraṃ haniṣyathaa tridhā bhūtaṃ kariṣye ham ātmānaṃ surasattamāḥc tena vṛtraṃ sahasrākṣo haniṣyati na saṃśayaḥa eko ṃśo vāsavaṃ yātu dvitīyo vajram eva tuc tṛtīyo bhūtalaṃ śakras tato vṛtraṃ haniṣyatia tathā bruvati deveśe devā vākyam athābruvanc evam etan na saṃdeho yathā vadasi daityahana bhadraṃ te stu gamiṣyāmo vṛtrāsuravadhaiṣiṇaḥc bhajasva paramodāravāsavaṃ svena tejasāa tataḥ sarve mahātmānaḥ sahasrākṣapurogamāḥc tad araṇyam upākrāman yatra vṛtro mahāsuraḥa te paśyaṃs tejasā bhūtaṃ tapantam asurottamamc pibantam iva lokāṃs trīn nirdahantam ivāmbarama dṛṣṭvaiva cāsuraśreṣṭhaṃ devās trāsam upāgamanc katham enaṃ vadhiṣyāmaḥ kathaṃ na syāt parājayaḥa teṣāṃ cintayatāṃ tatra sahasrākṣaḥ puraṃdaraḥc vajraṃ pragṛhya bāhubhyāṃ prahiṇod vṛtramūrdhania kālāgnineva ghoreṇa dīpteneva mahārciṣāc prataptaṃ vṛtraśirasi jagat trāsam upāgamata asaṃbhāvyaṃ vadhaṃ tasya vṛtrasya vibudhādhipaḥc cintayāno jagāmāśu lokasyāntaṃ mahāyaśāḥa tam indraṃ brahmahatyāśu gacchantam anugacchatic apatac cāsya gātreṣu tam indraṃ duḥkham āviśata hatārayaḥ pranaṣṭendrā devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥc viṣṇuṃ tribhuvaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ muhur muhur apūjayana tvaṃ gatiḥ paramā deva pūrvajo jagataḥ prabhuḥc rathārthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viṣṇutvam upajagmivāna hataś cāyaṃ tvayā vṛtro brahmahatyā ca vāsavamc bādhate suraśārdūla mokṣaṃ tasya vinirdiśaa teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devānāṃ viṣṇur abravītc mām eva yajatāṃ śakraḥ pāvayiṣyāmi vajriṇama puṇyena hayamedhena mām iṣṭvā pākaśāsanaḥc punar eṣyati devānām indratvam akutobhayaḥa evaṃ saṃdiśya devānāṃ tāṃ vāṇīm amṛtopamāc jagāma viṣṇur deveśaḥ stūyamānas triviṣṭapama tathā vṛtravadhaṃ sarvam akhilena sa lakṣmaṇaḥc kathayitvā naraśreṣṭhaḥ kathāśeṣam upākramata tato hate mahāvīrye vṛtre devabhayaṃkarec brahmahatyāvṛtaḥ śakraḥ saṃjñāṃ lebhe na vṛtrahāa so ntam āśritya lokānāṃ naṣṭasaṃjño vicetanaḥc kālaṃ tatrāvasat kaṃ cid veṣṭamāno yathoragaḥa atha naṣṭe sahasrākṣe udvignam abhavaj jagatc bhūmiś ca dhvastasaṃkāśā niḥsnehā śuṣkakānanāa niḥsrotasaś cāmbuvāhā hradāś ca saritas tathāc saṃkṣobhaś caiva sattvānām anāvṛṣṭikṛto bhavata kṣīyamāṇe tu loke smin saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ surāḥc yad uktaṃ viṣṇunā pūrvaṃ taṃ yajñaṃ samupānayana tataḥ sarve suragaṇāḥ sopādhyāyāḥ saharṣibhiḥc taṃ deśaṃ sahitā jagmur yatrendro bhayamohitaḥa te tu dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaṃ mohitaṃ brahmahatyayāc taṃ puraskṛtya deveśam aśvamedhaṃ pracakrirea tato śvamedhaḥ sumahān mahendrasya mahātmanaḥc vavṛdhe brahmahatyāyāḥ pāvanārthaṃ nareśvaraa tato yajñasamāptau tu brahmahatyā mahātmanaḥc abhigamyābravīd vākyaṃ kva me sthānaṃ vidhāsyathaa te tām ūcus tato devās tuṣṭāḥ prītisamanvitāḥc caturdhā vibhajātmānam ātmanaiva durāsadea devānāṃ bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā brahmahatyā mahātmanāmc saṃnidhau sthānam anyatra varayām āsa durvasāa ekenāṃśena vatsyāmi pūrṇodāsu nadīṣu vaic dvitīyena tu vṛkṣeṣu satyam etad bravīmi vaḥa yo yam aṃśas tṛtīyo me strīṣu yauvanaśāliṣuc trirātraṃ darpaparṇāsu vasiṣye darpaghātinīa hantāro brāhmaṇān ye tu prekṣāpūrvam adūṣakānc tāṃś caturthena bhāgena saṃśrayiṣye surarṣabhāḥa pratyūcus tāṃ tato devā yathā vadasi durvasec tathā bhavatu tat sarvaṃ sādhayasva yathepsitama tataḥ prītyānvitā devāḥ sahasrākṣaṃ vavandirec vijvaraḥ pūtapāpmā ca vāsavaḥ samapadyataa praśāntaṃ ca jagat sarvaṃ sahasrākṣe pratiṣṭhatec yajñaṃ cādbhutasaṃkāśaṃ tadā śakro bhyapūjayata īdṛśo hy aśvamedhasya prabhāvo raghunandanac yajasva sumahābhāga hayamedhena pārthivaa tac chrutvā lakṣmaṇenoktaṃ vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥc pratyuvāca mahātejāḥ prahasan rāghavo vacaḥa evam etan naraśreṣṭha yathā vadasi lakṣmaṇac vṛtraghātam aśeṣeṇa vājimedhaphalaṃ ca yata śrūyate hi purā saumya kardamasya prajāpateḥc putro bāhlīśvaraḥ śrīmān ilo nāma sudhārmikaḥa sa rājā pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ vaśe kṛtvā mahāyaśāḥc rājyaṃ caiva naravyāghra putravat paryapālayata suraiś ca paramodārair daiteyaiś ca mahāsuraiḥc nāgarākṣasagandharvair yakṣaiś ca sumahātmabhiḥa pūjyate nityaśaḥ saumya bhayārtai raghunandanac abibhyaṃś ca trayo lokāḥ saroṣasya mahātmanaḥa sa rājā tādṛśo hy āsīd dharme vīrye ca niṣṭhitaḥc buddhyā ca paramodāro bāhlīkānāṃ mahāyaśāḥa sa pracakre mahābāhur mṛgayāṃ rucire vanec caitre manorame māsi sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥa prajaghne sa nṛpo raṇye mṛgāñ śatasahasraśaḥc hatvaiva tṛptir nābhūc ca rājñas tasya mahātmanaḥa nānāmṛgāṇām ayutaṃ vadhyamānaṃ mahātmanāc yatra jāto mahāsenas taṃ deśam upacakramea tasmiṃs tu devadeveśaḥ śailarājasutāṃ haraḥc ramayām āsa durdharṣaiḥ sarvair anucaraiḥ sahaa kṛtvā strībhūtam ātmānam umeśo gopatidhvajaḥc devyāḥ priyacikīrṣuḥ sa tasmin parvatanirjharea ye ca tatra vanoddeśe sattvāḥ puruṣavādinaḥc yac ca kiṃ cana tat sarvaṃ nārīsaṃjñaṃ babhūva haa etasminn antare rājā sa ilaḥ kardamātmajaḥc nighnan mṛgasahasrāṇi taṃ deśam upacakramea sa dṛṣṭvā strīkṛtaṃ sarvaṃ savyālamṛgapakṣiṇamc ātmānaṃ sānugaṃ caiva strībhūtaṃ raghunandanaa tasya duḥkhaṃ mahat tv āsīd dṛṣṭvātmānaṃ tathā gatamc umāpateś ca tat karma jñātvā trāsam upāgamata tato devaṃ mahātmānaṃ śitikaṇṭhaṃ kapardinamc jagāma śaraṇaṃ rājā sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥa tataḥ prahasya varadaḥ saha devyā mahāyaśāḥc prajāpatisutaṃ vākyam uvāca varadaḥ svayama uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha rājarṣe kārdameya mahābalac puruṣatvam ṛte saumya varaṃ varaya suvrataa tataḥ sa rājā śokārtāḥ pratyākhyāto mahātmanāc na sa jagrāha strībhūto varam anyaṃ surottamāta tataḥ śokena mahatā śailarājasutāṃ nṛpaḥc praṇipatya mahādevīṃ sarveṇaivāntarātmanāa īśe varāṇāṃ varade lokānām asi bhāminic amoghadarśane devi bhaje saumye namo stu tea hṛdgataṃ tasya rājarṣer vijñāya harasaṃnidhauc pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ devī rudrasya saṃmatāa ardhasya devo varado varārdhasya tathā hy ahamc tasmād ardhaṃ gṛhāṇa tvaṃ strīpuṃsor yāvad icchasia tad adbhutatamaṃ śrutvā devyā varam anuttamamc saṃprahṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā rājā vākyam athābravīta yadi devi prasannā me rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvic māsaṃ strītvam upāsitvā māsaṃ syāṃ puruṣaḥ punaḥa īpsitaṃ tasya vijñāya devī surucirānanāc pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyam evam etad bhaviṣyatia rājan puruṣabhūtas tvaṃ strībhāvaṃ na smariṣyasic strībhūtaś cāparaṃ māsaṃ na smariṣyasi pauruṣama evaṃ sa rājā puruṣo māmaṃ bhūtvātha kārdamiḥc trailokyasundarī nārī māsam ekam ilābhavata tāṃ kathām ilasaṃbaddhāṃ rāmeṇa samudīritāmc lakṣmaṇo bharataś caiva śrutvā paramavismitaua tau rāmaṃ prāñjalībhūtvā tasya rājño mahātmanaḥc vistaraṃ tasya bhāvasya tadā papracchatuḥ punaḥa kathaṃ sa rājā strībhūto vartayām āsa durgatimc puruṣo vā yadā bhūtaḥ kāṃ vṛttiṃ vartayaty asaua tayos tad bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā kautūhalasamanvitamc kathayām āsa kākutṣṭhas tasya rājño yathā gatama tam eva prathamaṃ māsaṃ strībhūtvā lokasundarīc tābhiḥ parivṛtā strībhir ye sya pūrvaṃ padānugāḥa tat kānanaṃ vigāhyāśu vijahre lokasundarīc drumagulmalatākīrṇaṃ padbhyāṃ padmadalekṣaṇāa vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi saṃtyaktvā vai samantataḥc parvatābhogavivare tasmin reme ilā tadāa atha tasmin vanoddeśe parvatasyāvidūrataḥc saraḥ suruciraprakhyaṃ nānāpakṣigaṇāyutama dadarśa sā ilā tasmin budhaṃ somasutaṃ tadāc jvalantaṃ svena vapuṣā pūrṇaṃ somam ivoditama tapantaṃ ca tapas tīvram ambhomadhye durāsadamc yaśak saraṃ kāmagamaṃ tāruṇye paryavasthitama sā taṃ jalāśayaṃ sarvaṃ kṣobhayām āsa vismitāc saha taiḥ pūra puruṣaiḥ strībhūtai raghunandanaa budhas tu tāṃ nirīkṣyaiva kāmabāṇābhipīḍitaḥc nopalebhe tadātmānaṃ cacāla ca tadāmbhasia ilāṃ nirīkṣamāṇaḥ sa trailokyābhyadhikāṃ śubhāmc cintāṃ samabhyatikrāmat kā nv iyaṃ devatādhikāa na devīṣu na nāgīṣu nāsurīṣv apsaraḥsu cac dṛṣṭapūrvā mayā kā cid rūpeṇaitena śobhitāa sadṛśīyaṃ mama bhaved yadi nānyaparigrahāc iti buddhiṃ samāsthāya jalāt sthalam upāgamata sa āśramaṃ samupāgamya catasraḥ pramadās tataḥc śabdāpayata dharmātmā tāś cainaṃ ca vavandirea sa tāḥ papraccha dharmātma kasyaiṣā lokasundarīc kimartham āgatā ceha satyam ākhyāta mācirama śubhaṃ tu tasya tadvākyaṃ madhuraṃ madhurākṣaramc śrutvā tu tāḥ striyaḥ sarvā ūcur madhurayā girāa asmākam eṣā suśroṇī prabhutve vartate sadāc apatiḥ kānanānteṣu sahāsmābhir aṭaty asaua tad vākyam avyaktapadaṃ tāsāṃ strīṇāṃ niśamya tuc vidyām āvartanīṃ puṇyām āvartayata sa dvijaḥa so rthaṃ viditvā nikhilaṃ tasya rājño yathāgatamc sarvā eva striyas tāś ca babhāṣe munipuṃgavaḥa atra kiṃ puruṣā bhadrā avasañ śailarodhasic vatsyathāsmin girau yūyam avakāśo vidhīyatāma mūlaputraphalaiḥ sarvā vartayiṣyatha nityadāc striyaḥ kimpuruṣān nāma bhartṝn samupalapsyathaa tāḥ śrutvā somaputrasya vācaṃ kiṃpuruṣīkṛtāḥc upāsāṃ cakrire śailaṃ bahvyas tā bahudhā tadāa śrutvā kimpuruṣotpattiṃ lakṣmaṇo bharatas tadāc āścaryam iti cābrūtām ubhau rāmaṃ janeśvarama atha rāmaḥ kathām etāṃ bhūya eva mahāyaśāḥc kathayām āsa dharmātmā prajāpatisutasya vaia sarvās tā vidrutā dṛṣṭvā kiṃnarīr ṛṣisattamaḥc uvāca rūpasaṃpannāṃ tāṃ striyaṃ prahasann ivaa somasyāhaṃ sudayitaḥ sutaḥ surucirānanec bhajasva māṃ varārohe bhaktyā snigdhena cakṣuṣāa tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śūnye svajanavarjitāc ilā suruciraprakhyaṃ pratyuvāca mahāgrahama ahaṃ kāmakarī saumya tavāsmi vaśavartinīc praśādhi māṃ somasuta yathecchasi tathā kurua tasyās tad adbhutaprakhyaṃ śrutvā harṣasamanvitaḥc sa vai kāmī saha tayā reme candramasaḥ sutaḥa budhasya mādhavo māsas tām ilāṃ rucirānanāmc gato ramayato tyarthaṃ kṣaṇavat tasya kāminaḥa atha māse tu saṃpūrṇe pūrṇendusadṛśānanaḥc prajāpatisutaḥ śrīmāñ śayane pratyabudhyataa so paśyat somajaṃ tatra tapyantaṃ salilāśayec ūrdhvabāhuṃ nirālambaṃ taṃ rājā pratyabhāṣataa bhagavan parvataṃ durgaṃ praviṣṭo smi sahānugaḥc na ca paśyāmi tat sainyaṃ kva nu te māmakā gatāḥa tac chrutvā tasya rājarṣer naṣṭasaṃjñasya bhāṣitamc pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ sāntvayan parayā girāa aśmavarṣeṇa mahatā bhṛtyās te vinipātitāḥc tvaṃ cāśramapade supto vātavarṣabhayārditaḥa samāśvasihi bhadraṃ te nirbhayo vigatajvaraḥc phalamūlāśano vīra vasa ceha yathāsukhama sa rājā tena vākyena pratyāśvasto mahāyaśāḥc pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ dīno bhṛtyajanakṣayāta tyakṣyāmy ahaṃ svakaṃ rājyaṃ nāhaṃ bhṛtyair vinā kṛtaḥc vartayeyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ brahman samanujñātum arhasia suto dharmaparo brahmañ jyeṣṭho mama mahāyaśāḥc śaśabindur iti khyātaḥ sa me rājyaṃ prapatsyatea na hi śakṣyāmy ahaṃ gatvā bhṛtyadārān sukhānvitānc prativaktuṃ mahātejaḥ kiṃ cid apy aśubhaṃ vacaḥa tathā bruvati rājendre budhaḥ paramam adbhutamc sāntvapūrvam athovāca vāsas ta iha rocatāma na saṃtāpas tvayā kāryaḥ kārdameya mahābalac saṃvatsaroṣitasyeha kārayiṣyāmi te hitama tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā budhasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥc vāsāya vidadhe buddhiṃ yad uktaṃ brahmavādināa māsaṃ sa strī tadā bhūtvā ramayaty aniśaṃ śubhāc māsaṃ puruṣabhāvena dharmabuddhiṃ cakāra saḥa tataḥ sa navame māsi ilā somasutātmajamc janayām āsa suśroṇī purūravasam ātmajama jātamātraṃ tu suśroṇī pitur haste nyaveśayatc budhasya samavarṇābham ilāputraṃ mahābalama budho pi puruṣībhūtaṃ samāśvāsya narādhipamc kathābhī ramayām āsa dharmayuktābhir ātmavāna tathoktavati rāme tu tasya janma tad adbhutamc uvāca lakṣmaṇo bhūyo bharataś ca mahāyaśāḥa sā priyā somaputrasya saṃvatsaram athoṣitāc akarot kiṃ naraśreṣṭha tat tvaṃ śaṃsitum arhasia tayos tad vākyamādhuryaṃ niśamya paripṛcchatoḥc rāmaḥ punar uvācemāṃ prajāpatisute kathāma puruṣatvaṃ gate śūre budhaḥ paramabuddhimānc saṃvartaṃ paramodāram ājuhāva mahāyaśāḥa cyavanaṃ bhṛguputraṃ ca muniṃ cāriṣṭaneminamc pramodanaṃ modakaraṃ tato durvāsasaṃ munima etān sarvān samānīya vākyajñas tattvadarśinaḥc uvāca sarvān suhṛdo dhairyeṇa susamāhitaḥa ayaṃ rājā mahābāhuḥ kardamasya ilaḥ sutaḥc jānītainaṃ yathā bhūtaṃ śreyo hy asya vidhīyatāma teṣāṃ saṃvadatām eva tam āśramam upāgamatc kardamaḥ sumahātejā dvijaiḥ saha mahātmabhiḥa pulastyaś ca kratuś caiva vaṣaṭkāras tathaiva cac oṃkāraś ca mahātejās tam āśramam upāgamana te sarve hṛṣṭamanasaḥ parasparasamāgamec hitaiṣiṇo bāhli pateḥ pṛthag vākyam athābruvana kardamas tv abravīd vākyaṃ sutārthaṃ paramaṃ hitamc dvijāḥ śṛṇuta madvākyaṃ yac chreyaḥ pārthivasya hia nānyaṃ paśyāmi bhaiṣajyam antareṇa vṛṣadhvajamc nāśvamedhāt paro yajñaḥ priyaś caiva mahātmanaḥa tasmād yajāmahe sarve pārthivārthe durāsadamc kardamenaivam uktās tu sarva eva dvijarṣabhāḥe rocayanti sma taṃ yajñaṃ rudrasyārādhanaṃ pratia saṃvartasya tu rājarṣiḥ śiṣyaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥc marutta iti vikhyatas taṃ yajñaṃ samupāharata tato yajño mahān āsīd budhāśramasamīpataḥc rudraś ca paramaṃ toṣam ājagāma mahāyaśāḥa atha yajñasamāptau tu prītaḥ paramayā mudāc umāpatir dvijān sarvān uvācedam ilāṃ pratia prīto smi hayamedhena bhaktyā ca dvijasattamāḥc asya bāhlipateś caiva kiṃ karomi priyaṃ śubhama tathā vadati deveśe dvijās te susamāhitāḥc prasādayanti deveśaṃ yathā syāt puruṣas tv ilāa tataḥ prītamanā rudraḥ puruṣatvaṃ dadau punaḥc ilāyai sumahātejā dattvā cāntaradhīyataa nivṛtte hayamedhe tu gate cādarśanaṃ harec yathāgataṃ dvijāḥ sarve agacchan dīrghadarśinaḥa rājā tu bāhlim utsṛjya madhyadeśe hy anuttamamc niveśayām āsa puraṃ pratiṣṭhānaṃ yaśaskarama śaśabindus tu rājāsīd bāhlyāṃ parapuraṃjayaḥc pratiṣṭhāna ilo rājā prajāpatisuto balīa sa kāle prāptavāṃl lokam ilo brāhmam anuttamamc ailaḥ purūravā rājā pratiṣṭhānam avāptavāna īdṛśo hy aśvamedhasya prabhāvaḥ puruṣarṣabhauc strībhūtaḥ pauruṣaṃ lebhe yac cānyad api durlabhama etad ākhyāya kākutstho bhrātṛhyām amitaprabhaḥc lakṣmaṇaṃ punār evāha dharmayuktam idaṃ vacaḥa vasiṣṭhaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca jābālim atha kaśyapamc dvijāṃś ca sarvapravarān aśvamedhapuraskṛtāna etān sarvān samāhūya mantrayitvā ca lakṣmaṇac hayaṃ lakṣmaṇasaṃpannaṃ vimokṣyāmi samādhināa tad vākyaṃ rāghaveṇoktaṃ śrutvā tvaritavikramaḥc dvijān sarvān samāhūya darśayām āsa rāghavama te dṛṣṭvā devasaṃkāśaṃ kṛtapādābhivandanamc rāghavaṃ sudurādharṣam āśīrbhiḥ samapūjayana prāñjalis tu tato bhūtvā rāghavo dvijasāttamānc uvāca dharmasaṃyuktam aśvamedhāśritaṃ vacaḥa sa teṣāṃ dvijamukhyānāṃ vākyam adbhutadarśanamc aśvamedhāśritaṃ śrutvā bhṛśaṃ prīto bhavat tadāa vijñāya tu mataṃ teṣāṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravītc preṣayasva mahābāho sugrīvāya mahātmanea śīghraṃ mahadbhir haribhir bahibhiś ca tadāśrayaiḥc sārdham āgaccha bhadraṃ te anubhoktuṃ makhottamama vibhīṣaṇaś ca rakṣobhiḥ kāmagair bahubhir vṛtaḥc aśvamedhaṃ mahābāhuḥ prāpnotu laghuvikramaḥa rājānaś ca naravyāghra ye me priyacikīrṣavaḥc sānugāḥ kṣipram āyāntu yajñabhūmim anuttamāma deśāntaragatā ye ca dvijā dharmaparāyaṇāḥc nimantrayasva tān sarvān aśvamedhāya lakṣmaṇaa ṛṣayaś cā mahābāho āhūyantāṃ tapodhanāḥc deśāntaragatā ye ca sadārāś ca maharṣayaḥa yajñavāṭaś ca sumahān gomatyā naimiṣe vanec ājñāpyatāṃ mahābāho tad dhi puṇyam anuttamama śataṃ vāhasahasrāṇāṃ taṇḍulānāṃ vapuṣmatāmc ayutaṃ tilamudgasya prayātv agre mahābalaa suvarṇakoṭyo bahulā hiraṇyasya śatottarāḥc agrato bharataḥ kṛtvā gacchatv agre mahāmatiḥa antarāpaṇavīthyaś ca sarvāṃś ca naṭanartakānc naigamān bālavṛddhāṃś ca dvijāṃś ca susamāhitāna karmāntikāṃś ca kuśalāñ śilpinaś ca supaṇḍitānc mātaraś caiva me sarvāḥ kumārāntaḥpurāṇi caa kāñcanīṃ mama patnīṃ ca dīkṣārhāṃ yajñakarmaṇic agrato bharataḥ kṛtvā gacchatv agre mahāmatiḥa tat sarvam akhilenāśu prasthāpya bharatāgrajaḥc hayaṃ lakṣmaṇasaṃpannaṃ kṛṣṇasāraṃ mumoca haa ṛtvigbhir lakṣmaṇaṃ sārdham aśve ca viniyujya saḥc tato bhyagacchat kākutsthaḥ saha sainyena naimiṣama yajñavāṭaṃ mahābāhur dṛṣṭvā paramam adbhutamc praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe śrīmān iti ca so bravīta naimiṣe vasatas tasya sarva eva narādhipāḥc ājagmuḥ sarvarāṣṭrebhyas tān rāmaḥ pratyapūjayata upakāryān mahārhāṃś ca pārthivānāṃ mahātmanāmc sānugānāṃ naraśreṣṭho vyādideśa mahādyutiḥa annapānāni vastrāṇi sānugānāṃ mahātmanāmc bharataḥ saṃdadāv āśu śatrughnasahitas tadāa vānarāś ca mahātmānaḥ sugrīvasahitās tadāc viprāṇāṃ praṇatāḥ sarve cakrire pariveṣaṇama vibhīṣaṇaś ca rakṣobhiḥ sragvibhir bahubhir vṛtaḥc ṛṣīṇām ugratapasāṃ kiṃkaraḥ paryupasthitaḥa evaṃ suvihito yajño hayamedho bhyavartatac lakṣmaṇenābhiguptā ca hayacaryā pravartitāa nānyaḥ śabdo bhavat tatra hayamedhe mahātmanaḥc chandato dehi visrabdho yāvat tuṣyanti yācakāḥe tāvad vānararakṣobhir dattam evābhyadṛśyataa na kaś cin malinas tatra dīno vāpy atha vā kṛśaḥc tasmin yajñavare rājño hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtea ye ca tatra mahātmāno munayaś cirajīvinaḥc nāsmaraṃs tādṛśaṃ yajñaṃ dānaughasamalaṃkṛtama rajatānāṃ suvarṇānāṃ ratnānām atha vāsasāmc aniśaṃ dīyamānānāṃ nāntaḥ samupadṛśyatea na śakrasya na somasya yamasya varuṇasya vāc īdṛśo dṛṣṭapūrvo na evam ūcus tapodhanāḥa sarvatra vānarās tasthuḥ sarvatraiva ca rākṣasāḥc vāso dhanāni kāmibhyaḥ pūrṇahastā dadur bhṛśama īdṛśo rājasiṃhasya yajñaḥ sarvaguṇānvitaḥc saṃvatsaram atho sāgraṃ vartate na ca hīyatea vartamāne tathābhūte yajñe paramake dbhutec saśiṣya ājagāmāśu vālmīkir munipuṃgavaḥa sa dṛṣṭvā divyasaṃkāśaṃ yajñam adbhutadarśanamc ekānte ṛṣivāṭānāṃ cakāra uṭajāñ śubhāna sa śiṣyāv abravīd dhṛṣṭo yuvāṃ gatvā samāhitauc kṛtsnaṃ rāmāyaṇaṃ kāvyaṃ gāyatāṃ parayā mudāa ṛṣivāṭeṣu puṇyeṣu brāhmaṇāvasatheṣu cac rathyāsu rājamārgeṣu pārthivānāṃ gṛheṣu caa rāmasya bhavanadvāri yatra karma ca vartatec ṛtvijām agrataś caiva tatra geyaṃ viśeṣataḥa imāni ca phalāny atra svādūni vividhāni cac jātāni parvatāgreṣu āsvādyāsvādya gīyatāma na yāsyathaḥ śramaṃ vatsau bhakṣayitvā phalāni vaic mūlāni ca sumṛṣṭāni nagarāt parihāsyathaa yadi śabdāpayed rāmaḥ śravaṇāya mahīpatiḥc ṛṣīṇām upaviṣṭānāṃ tato geyaṃ pravartatāma divase viṃśatiḥ sargā geyā vai parayā mudāc pramāṇair bahubhis tatra yathoddiṣṭaṃ mayā purāa lobhaś cāpi na kartavyaḥ svalpo pi dhanakāṅkṣayāc kiṃ dhanenāśramasthānāṃ phalamūlopabhogināma yadi pṛcchet sa kākutstho yuvāṃ kasyeti dārakauc vālmīker atha śiṣyau hi brūtām evaṃ narādhipama imās tantrīḥ sumadhurāḥ sthānaṃ vā pūrvadarśitamc mūrchayitvā sumadhuraṃ gāyetāṃ vigatajvaraua ādiprabhṛti geyaṃ syān na cāvajñāya pārthivamc pitā hi sarvabhūtānāṃ rājā bhavati dharmataḥa tad yuvāṃ hṛṣṭamanasau śvaḥ prabhāte samādhināc gāyetāṃ madhuraṃ geyaṃ tantrīlayasamanvitama iti saṃdiśya bahuśo muniḥ prācetasas tadāc vālmīkiḥ paramodāras tūṣṇīm āsīn mahāyaśāḥa tām adbhutāṃ tau hṛdaye kumārauniveśya vāṇīm ṛṣibhāṣitāṃ śubhāmc samutsukau tau sukham ūṣatur niśāṃyathāśvinau bhārgavanītisaṃskṛtaua tau rajanyāṃ prabhātāyāṃ snātau hutahutāśanauc yathoktam ṛṣiṇā pūrvaṃ tatra tatrābhyagāyatāma tāṃ sa śuśrāva kākutsthaḥ pūrvacaryāṃ tatas tataḥc apūrvāṃ pāṭhya jātiṃ ca geyena samalaṃkṛtāma pramāṇair bahubhir baddhāṃ tantrīlayasamanvitāmc bālābhyāṃ rāghavaḥ śrutvā kautūhalaparo bhavata atha karmāntare rājā samānīya mahāmunīnc pārthivāṃś ca naravyāghraḥ paṇḍitān naigamāṃs tathāa paurāṇikāñ śabdavito ye ca vṛddhā dvijātayaḥc etān sarvān samānīya gātārau samaveśayata hṛṣṭā ṛṣigaṇās tatra pārthivāś ca mahaujasaḥc pibanta iva cakṣurbhyāṃ rājānaṃ gāyakau ca taua parasparam athocus te sarva eva samaṃ tataḥc ubhau rāmasya sadṛśau bimbād bimbam ivoddhṛtaua jaṭilau yadi na syātāṃ na valkaladharau yadic viśeṣaṃ nādhigacchāmo gāyato rāghavasya caa teṣāṃ saṃvadatām evaṃ śrotṝṇāṃ harṣavardhanamc geyaṃ pracakratus tatra tāv ubhau munidārakaua tataḥ pravṛttaṃ madhuraṃ gāndharvam atimānuṣamc na ca tṛptiṃ yayuḥ sarve śrotāro geya saṃpadāa pravṛttam āditaḥ pūrvaṃ sargān nāradadarśanātc tataḥ prabhṛti sargāṃś ca yāvadviṃśaty agāyatāma tato parāhṇasamaye rāghavaḥ samabhāṣatac śrutvā viṃśatisargāṃs tān bharataṃ bhrātṛvatsalaḥa aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi suvarṇasya mahātmanoḥc dadasva śīghraṃ kākutstha bālayor mā vṛthā śramaḥa dīyamānaṃ suvarṇaṃ tan nāgṛhṇītāṃ kuśīlavauc ūcatuś ca mahātmānau kim aneneti vismitaua vanyena phalamūlena niratu svo vanaukasauc suvarṇena hiraṇyena kiṃ kariṣyāvahe vanea tathā tayoḥ prabruvatoḥ kautūhalasamanvitāḥc śrotāraś caiva rāmaś ca sarva eva suvismitāḥa tasya caivāgamaṃ rāmaḥ kāvyasya śrotum utsukaḥc papraccha tau mahātejās tāv ubhau munidārakaua kiṃpramāṇam idaṃ kāvyaṃ kā pratiṣṭhā mahātmanaḥc kartā kāvyasya mahataḥ ko vāsau munipuṃgavaḥa pṛcchantaṃ rāghavaṃ vākyam ūcatur munidārakauc vālmīkir bhagavān kartā saṃprāpto yajñasaṃnidhime yenedaṃ caritaṃ tubhyam aśeṣaṃ saṃpradarśitama ādiprabhṛti rājendra pañcasarga śatāni cac pratiṣṭhā jīvitaṃ yāvat tāvad rājañ śubhāśubhama yadi buddhiḥ kṛtā rājañ śravaṇāya mahārathac karmāntare kṣaṇī hūtas tac chṛṇuṣva sahānujaḥa bāḍham ity abravīd rāmas tau cānujñāpya rāghavamc prahṛṣṭau jagmatur vāsaṃ yatrāsau munipuṃgavaḥa rāmo pi munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ pārthivaiś ca mahātmabhiḥc śrutvā tad gītamādhuryaṃ karmaśālām upāgamata rāmo bahūny ahāny eva tad gītaṃ paramādbhutamc śuśrāva munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ rājabhiḥ saha vānaraiḥa tasmin gīte tu vijñāya sītāputrau kuśīlavauc tasyāḥ pariṣado madhye rāmo vacanam abravīta madvaco brūta gacchadhvam iti bhagavato ntikama yadi śuddhasamācārā yadi vā vītakalmaṣāc karotv ihātmanaḥ śuddhim anumānya mahāmunima chandaṃ munes tu vijñāya sītāyāś ca manogatamc pratyayaṃ dātukāmāyās tataḥ śaṃsata me laghua śvaḥ prabhāte tu śapathaṃ maithilī janakātmajāc karotu pariṣanmadhye śodhanārthaṃ mameha caa śrutvā tu rāghavasyaitad vacaḥ paramam adbhutamc dūtāḥ saṃprayayur vāṭaṃ yatrāste munipuṃgavaḥa te praṇamya mahātmānaṃ jvalantam amitaprabhamc ūcus te rāma vākyāni mṛdūni madhurāṇi caa teṣāṃ tad bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā rāmasya ca manogatamc vijñāya sumahātejā munir vākyam athābravīta evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ vo yathā tuṣyati rāghavaḥc tathā kariṣyate sītā daivataṃ hi patiḥ striyāḥa tathoktā muninā sarve rāmadūtā mahaujasaḥc pratyetya rāghavaṃ sarve munivākyaṃ babhāṣirea tataḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ kākutsthaḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ mahātmanaḥc ṛṣīṃs tatra sametāṃś ca rājñaś caivābhyabhāṣataa bhagavantaḥ saśiṣyā vai sānugaś ca narādhipāḥc paśyantu sītāśapathaṃ yaś caivānyo bhikāṅkṣatea tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāghavasya mahātmanaḥc sarveṣam ṛṣimukhyānāṃ sādhuvādo mahān abhūta rājānaś ca mahātmānaḥ praśaṃsanti sma rāghavamc upapannaṃ naraśreṣṭha tvayy eva bhuvi nānyataḥa evaṃ viniścayaṃ kṛtvā śvobhūta iti rāghavaḥc visarjayām āsa tadā sarvāṃs tāñ śatrusūdanaḥa tasyāṃ rajanyāṃ vyuṣṭāyāṃ yajñavāṭagato nṛpaḥc ṛṣīn sarvān mahātejāḥ śabdāpayati rāghavaḥa vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābālir atha kāśyapaḥc viśvāmitro dīrghatapā durvāsāś ca mahātapāḥa agastyo tha tathāśaktir bhārgavaś caiva vāmanaḥc mārkaṇḍeyaś ca dīrghāyur maudgalyaś ca mahātapāḥa bhārgavaś cyavanaś caiva śatānandaś ca dharmavitc bharadvājaś ca tejasvī agniputraś ca suprabhaḥa ete cānye ca munayo bahavaḥ saṃśitavratāḥc rājānaś ca naravyāghrāḥ sarva eva samāgatāḥa rākṣasāś ca mahāvīryā vānarāś ca mahābalāḥc samājagmur mahātmānaḥ sarva eva kutūhalāta kṣatriyāś caiva vaiśyāś ca śūdrāś caiva sahasraśaḥc sītāśapathavīkṣārthaṃ sarva eva samāgatāḥa tathā samāgataṃ sarvam aśvabhūtam ivācalamc śrutvā munivaras tūrṇaṃ sasītaḥ samupāgamata tam ṛṣiṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ sītā sānvagacchad avāṅmukhīc kṛtāñjalir bāṣpagalā kṛtvā rāmaṃ manogatama tāṃ dṛṣṭvā śrīm ivāyāntīṃ brahmāṇam anugāminīmc vālmīkeḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ sītāṃ sādhukāro mahān abhūta tato halahalā śabdaḥ sarveṣām evam ābabhauc duḥkhajena viśālena śokenākulitātmanāma sādhu sīteti ke cit tu sādhu rāmeti cāparec ubhāv eva tu tatrānye sādhu sādhv iti cābruvana tato madhyaṃ janaughānāṃ praviśya munipuṃgavaḥc sītāsahāyo vālmīkir iti hovāca rāghavama iyaṃ dāśarathe sītā suvratā dharmacāriṇīc apāpā te parityaktā mamāśramasamīpataḥa lokāpavādabhītasya tava rāma mahāvratac pratyayaṃ dāsyate sītā tām anujñātum arhasia imau ca jānakī putrāv ubhau ca yamajātakauc sutau tavaiva durdharṣo satyam etad bravīmi tea pracetaso haṃ daśamaḥ putro rāghavanandanac na smarāmy anṛtaṃ vākyaṃ tathemau tava putrakaua bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi tapaścaryā mayā kṛtāc tasyāḥ phalam upāśnīyām apāpā maithilī yathāa ahaṃ pañcasu bhūteṣu manaḥṣaṣṭheṣu rāghavac vicintya sītāṃ śuddheti nyagṛhṇāṃ vananirjharea iyaṃ śuddhasamācārā apāpā patidevatāc lokāpavādabhītasya dāsyati pratyayaṃ tavaa vālmīkinaivam uktas tu rāghavaḥ pratyabhāṣatac prāñjalir jagato madhye dṛṣṭvā tāṃ devavarṇinīma evam etan mahābhāga yathā vadasi dharmavitc pratyayo hi mama brahmaṃs tava vākyair akalmaṣaiḥa pratyayo hi purā datto vaidehyā surasaṃnidhauc seyaṃ lokabhayād brahmann apāpety abhijānatāe parityaktā mayā sītā tad bhavān kṣantum arhatia jānāmi cemau putrau me yamajātau kuśīlavauc śuddhāyāṃ jagato madhye maithilyāṃ prītir astu mea abhiprāyaṃ tu vijñāya rāmasya surasattamāḥc pitāmahaṃ puraskṛtya sarva eva samāgatāḥa ādityā vasavo rudrā viśve deśā marudgaṇāḥc aśvināv ṛṣigandharvā apsarāṇāṃ gaṇās tathāe sādhyāś ca devāḥ sarve te sarve ca paramarṣayaḥa tato vāyuḥ śubhaḥ puṇyo divyagandho manoramaḥc taṃ janaughaṃ suraśreṣṭho hlādayām āsa sarvataḥa tad adbhutam ivācintyaṃ nirīkṣante samāhitāḥc mānavāḥ sarvarāṣṭrebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ kṛtayuge yathāa sarvān samāgatān dṛṣṭvā sītā kāṣāyavāsinīc abravīt prāñjalir vākyam adhodṛṣṭir avānmukhīa yathāhaṃ rāghavād anyaṃ manasāpi na cintayec tathā me mādhavī devī vivaraṃ dātum arhatia tathā śapantyāṃ vaidehyāṃ prādurāsīt tad adbhutamc bhūtalād utthitaṃ divyaṃ siṃhāsanam anuttamama dhriyamāṇaṃ śirobhis tan nāgair amitavikramaiḥc divyaṃ divyena vapuṣā sarvaratnavibhūṣitama tasmiṃs tu dharaṇī devī bāhubhyāṃ gṛhya maithilīmc svāgatenābhinandyainām āsane copaveṣayata tām āsanagatāṃ dṛṣṭvā praviśantīṃ rasātalamc puṇyavṛṣṭir avicchinnā divyā sītām avākirata sādhukāraś ca sumahān devānāṃ sahasotthitaḥc sādhu sādhv iti vai sīte yasyās te śīlam īdṛśama evaṃ bahuvidhā vāco hy antarikṣagatāḥ surāḥc vyājahrur hṛṣṭamanaso dṛṣṭvā sītāpraveśanama yajñavāṭagatāś cāpi munayaḥ sarva eva tec rājānaś ca naravyāghrā vismayān noparemirea antarikṣe ca bhūmau ca sarve sthāvarajaṅgamāḥc dānavāś ca mahākāyāḥ pātāle pannagādhipāḥa ke cid vineduḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ ke cid dhyānaparāyaṇāḥc ke cid rāmaṃ nirīkṣante ke cit sītām acetanāḥa sītāpraveśanaṃ dṛṣṭvā teṣām āsīt samāgamaḥc taṃ muhūrtam ivātyarthaṃ sarvaṃ saṃmohitaṃ jagata tadāvasāne yajñasya rāmaḥ paramadurmanāḥc apaśyamāno vaidehīṃ mene śūnyam idaṃ jagate śokena paramāyatto na śāntiṃ manasāgamata visṛjya pārthivān sarvān ṛkṣavānararākṣasānc janaughaṃ brahmamukhyānāṃ vittapūrṇaṃ vyasarjayata tato visṛjya tān sarvān rāmo rājīvalocanaḥc hṛdi kṛtvā tadā sītām ayodhyāṃ praviveśa saḥa na sītāyāḥ parāṃ bhāryāṃ vavre sa raghunandanaḥc yajñe yajñe ca patnyarthaṃ jānakī kāñcanī bhavata daśavarṣasahasrāṇi vājimedham upākarotc vājapeyān daśaguṇāṃs tathā bahusuvarṇakāna agniṣṭomātirātrābhyāṃ gosavaiś ca mahādhanaiḥc īje kratubhir anyaiś ca sa śrīmān āptadakṣiṇaiḥa evaṃ sa kālaḥ sumahān rājyasthasya mahātmanaḥc dharme prayatamānasya vyatīyād rāghavasya tua ṛkṣavānararakṣāṃsi sthitā rāmasya śāsanec anurajyanti rājāno ahany ahani rāghavama kāle varṣati parjanyaḥ subhikṣaṃ vimalā diśaḥc hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇaṃ puraṃ janapadas tathāa nākāle mriyate kaś cin na vyādhiḥ prāṇināṃ tadāc nādharmaś cābhavat kaś cid rāme rājyaṃ praśāsatia atha dīrghasya kālasya rāmamātā yaśasvinīc putrapautraiḥ parivṛtā kāladharmam upāgamata anviyāya sumitrāpi kaikeyī ca yaśasvinīc dharmaṃ kṛtvā bahuvidhaṃ tridive paryavasthitāa sarvāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ svarge rājñā daśarathena cac samāgatā mahābhāgāḥ saha dharmaṃ ca lebhirea tāsāṃ rāmo mahādānaṃ kāle kāle prayacchatic mātṝṇām aviśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇeṣu tapasviṣua pitryāṇi bahuratnāni yajñān paramadustarānc cakāra rāmo dharmātmā pitṝn devān vivardhayana kasya cit tv atha kālasya yudhājit kekayo nṛpaḥc svaguruṃ preṣayām āsa rāghavāya mahātmanea gārgyam aṅgirasaḥ putraṃ brahmarṣim amitaprabhamc daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi prītidānam anuttamama kambalāni ca ratnāni citravastram athottamamc rāmāya pradadau rājā bahūny ābharaṇāni caa śrutvā tu rāghavo gārgyaṃ maharṣiṃ samupāgatamc mātulasyāśvapatinaḥ priyaṃ dūtam upāgatama pratyudgamya ca kākutsthaḥ krośamātraṃ sahānugaḥc gārgyaṃ saṃpūjayām āsa dhanaṃ tat pratigṛhya caa pṛṣṭvā ca prītidaṃ sarvaṃ kuśalaṃ mātulasya cac upaviṣṭaṃ mahābhāgaṃ rāmaḥ praṣṭuṃ pracakramea kim āha matulo vākyaṃ yadarthaṃ bhagavān ihac prāpto vākyavidāṃ śreṣṭha sākṣād iva bṛhaspatiḥa rāmasya bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā brahmarṣiḥ kāryavistaramc vaktum adbhutasaṃkāśaṃ rāghavāyopacakramea mātulas te mahābāho vākyam āha nararṣabhac yudhājit prītisaṃyuktaṃ śrūyatāṃ yadi rocatea ayaṃ gandharvaviṣayaḥ phalamūlopaśobhitaḥc sindhor ubhayataḥ pārśve deśaḥ paramaśobhanaḥa taṃ ca rakṣanti gandharvāḥ sāyudhā yuddhakovidāḥc śailūṣasya sutā vīrās tisraḥ koṭyo mahābalāḥa tān vinirjitya kākutstha gandharvaviṣayaṃ śubhamc niveśaya mahābāho dve pure susamāhitaḥa anyasya na gatis tatra deśaś cāyaṃ suśobhanaḥc rocatāṃ te mahābāho nāhaṃ tvām anṛtaṃ vadea tac chrutvā rāghavaḥ prīto mararṣir mātulasya cac uvāca bāḍham ity evaṃ bharataṃ cānvavaikṣataa so bravīd rāghavaḥ prītaḥ prāñjalipragraho dvijamc imau kumārau taṃ deśaṃ brahmarṣe vijayiṣyataḥa bharatasyātmajau vīrau takṣaḥ puṣkala eva cac mātulena suguptau tau dharmeṇa ca samāhitaua bharataṃ cāgrataḥ kṛtvā kumārau sabalānugauc nihatya gandharvasutān dve pure vibhajiṣyataḥa niveśya te puravare ātmājau saṃniveśya cac āgamiṣyati me bhūyaḥ sakāśam atidhārmikaḥa brahmarṣim evam uktvā tu bharataṃ sabalānugamc ājñāpayām āsa tadā kumārau cābhyaṣecayata nakṣatreṇa ca saumyena puraskṛtyāṅgiraḥ sutamc bharataḥ saha sainyena kumārābhyāṃ ca niryayaua sā senā śakrayukteva naragān niryayāv athac rāghavānugatā dūraṃ durādharṣā surāsuraiḥa māṃsāśīni ca sattvāni rakṣāṃsi sumahānti cac anujagmuś ca bharataṃ rudhirasya pipāsayāa bhūtagrāmāś ca bahavo māṃsabhakṣāḥ sudāruṇāḥc gandharvaputramāṃsāni bhoktukāmāḥ sahasraśaḥa siṃhavyāghrasṛgālānāṃ khecarāṇāṃ ca pakṣiṇāmc bahūni vai sahasrāṇi senāyā yayur agrataḥa adhyardhamāsam uṣitā pathi senā nirāmayāc hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇā kekayaṃ samupāgamata śrutvā senāpatiṃ prāptaṃ bharataṃ kekayādhipaḥc yudhājid gārgyasahitaṃ parāṃ prītim upāgamata sa niryayau janaughena mahatā kekayādhipaḥc tvaramāṇo bhicakrāma gandharvān devarūpiṇaḥa bharataś ca yudhājic ca sametau laghuvikramauc gandharvanagaraṃ prāptau sabalau sapadānugaua śrutvā tu bharataṃ prāptaṃ gandharvās te samāgatāḥc yoddhukāmā mahāvīryā vinadantaḥ samantataḥa tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc saptarātraṃ mahābhīmaṃ na cānyatarayor jayaḥa tato rāmānujaḥ kruddhaḥ kālasyāstraṃ sudāruṇamc saṃvartaṃ nāma bharato gandharveṣv abhyayojayata te baddhāḥ kālapāśena saṃvartena vidāritāḥc kṣaṇenābhihatās tisras tatra koṭyo mahātmanāa taṃ ghātaṃ ghorasaṃkāśaṃ na smaranti divaukasaḥc nimeṣāntaramātreṇa tādṛśānāṃ mahātmanāma hateṣu teṣu vīreṣu bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥc niveśayām āsa tadā samṛddhe dve purottamee takṣaṃ takṣaśilāyāṃ tu puṣkaraṃ puṣkarāvataua gandharvadeśo ruciro gāndhāraviṣayaś ca saḥc varṣaiḥ pañcabhir ākīrṇo viṣayair nāgarais tathāa dhanaratnaughasaṃpūrṇo kānanair upaśobhitec anyonyasaṃgharṣakṛte spardhayā guṇavistarea ubhe suruciraprakhye vyavahārair akalmaṣaiḥc udyānayānaughavṛte suvibhaktāntarāpaṇea ubhe puravare ramye vistarair upaśobhitec gṛhamukhyaiḥ surucirair vimānaiḥ samavarṇibhiḥa śobhite śobhanīyaiś ca devāyatanavistaraiḥc niveśya pañcabhir varṣair bharato rāghavānujaḥe punar āyān mahābāhur ayodhyāṃ kaikayīsutaḥa so bhivādya mahātmānaṃ sākṣād dharmam ivāparamc rāghavaṃ bharataḥ śrīmān brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥa śaśaṃsa ca yathāvṛttaṃ gandharvavadham uttamamc niveśanaṃ ca deśasya śrutvā prīto sya rāghavaḥa tac chrutvā harṣam āpede rāghavo bhrātṛbhiḥ sahac vākyaṃ cādbhutasaṃkāśaṃ bhrātṝn provāca rāghavaḥa imau kumārau saumitre tava dharmaviśāradauc aṅgadaś candraketuś ca rājyārhau dṛḍhadhanvinaua imau rājye bhiṣekṣyāmi deśaḥ sādhu vidhīyatāmc ramaṇīyo hy asaṃbādho rametāṃ yatra dhanvinaua na rājñāṃ yatra pīdā syān nāśramāṇāṃ vināśanamc sa deśo dṛśyatāṃ saumya nāparādhyāmahe yathāa tathoktavati rāme tu bharataḥ pratyuvāca hac ayaṃ kārāpatho deśaḥ suramaṇyo nirāmayaḥa niveśyatāṃ tatra puram aṅgadasya mahātmanaḥc candraketoś ca ruciraṃ candrakāntaṃ nirāmayama tad vākyaṃ bharatenoktaṃ pratijagrāha rāghavaḥc taṃ ca kṛtā vaśe deśam aṅgadasya nyaveśayata aṅgadīyā purī ramyā aṅgadasya niveśitāc ramaṇīyā suguptā ca rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇāa candraketus tu mallasya mallabhūmyāṃ niveśitāc candrakānteti vikhyātā divyā svargapurī yathāa tato rāmaḥ parāṃ prītiṃ bharato lakṣmaṇas tathāc yayur yudhi durādharṣā abhiṣekaṃ ca cakrirea abhiṣicya kumārau dvau prasthāpya sabalānugauc aṅgadaṃ paścimā bhūmiṃ candraketum udaṅmukhama aṅgadaṃ cāpi saumitrir lakṣmaṇo nujagāma hac candraketos tu bharataḥ pārṣṇigrāho babhūva haa lakṣmaṇas tv aṅgadīyāyāṃ saṃvatsaram athoṣitaḥc putre sthite durādharṣe ayodhyāṃ punar āgamata bharato pi tathaivoṣya saṃvatsaram athādhikamc ayodhyāṃ punar agamya rāmapādāv upāgamata ubhau saumitribharatau rāmapādāv anuvratauc kālaṃ gatam api snehān na jajñāte tidhārmikaua evaṃ varṣasahasrāṇi daśateṣāṃ yayus tadāc dharme prayatamānānāṃ paurakāryeṣu nityadāa vihṛtya lākaṃ paripūrṇamānasāḥśriyā vṛtā dharmapathe pare sthitāḥc trayaḥ samiddhā iva dīptatejasāhutāgnayaḥ sādhu mahādhvare trayaḥa kasya cit tv atha kālasya rāme dharmapathe sthitec kālas tāpasarūpeṇa rājadvāram upāgamata so bravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ dhṛtimantaṃ yaśasvinamc māṃ nivedaya rāmāya saṃprāptaṃ kāryagauravāta dūto hy atibalasyāhaṃ maharṣer amitaujasaḥc rāmaṃ didṛkṣur āyātaḥ kāryeṇa hi mahābalaa tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā saumitris tvarayānvitaḥc nyavedayata rāmāya tāpasasya vivakṣitama jayasva rājan dharmeṇa ubhau lokau mahādyutec dūtas tvāṃ draṣṭum āyātas tapasvī bhāskaraprabhaḥa tad vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇenoktaṃ śrutvā rāma uvāca hac praveśyatāṃ munis tāta mahaujās tasya vākyadhṛka saumitris tu tathety uktvā prāveśayata taṃ munimc jvalantam iva tejobhiḥ pradahantam ivāṃśubhiḥa so bhigamya raghuśreṣṭhaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasāc ṛṣir madhurayā vācā vardhasvety āha rāghavama tasmai rāmo mahātejāḥ pūjām arghya purogamāmc dadau kuśalam avyagraṃ praṣṭuṃ caivopacakramea pṛṣṭhaś ca kuśalaṃ tena rāmeṇa vadatāṃ varaḥc āsane kāñcane divye niṣasāda mahāyaśāḥa tam uvāca tato rāmaḥ svāgataṃ te mahāmunec prāpayasva ca vākyāni yato dūtas tvam āgataḥa codito rājasiṃhena munir vākyam udīrayatc dvandvam etat pravaktavyaṃ na ca cakṣur hataṃ vacaḥa yaḥ śṛṇoti nirīkṣed vā sa vadhyas tava rāghavac bhaved vai munimukhyasya vacanaṃ yady avekṣasea tatheti ca pratijñāya rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravītc dvāri tiṣṭha mahābāho pratihāraṃ visarjayaa sa me vadhyaḥ khalu bhavet kathāṃ dvandvasamīritāmc ṛṣer mama ca saumitre paśyed vā śṛṇuyā ca yaḥa tato nikṣipya kākutstho lakṣmaṇaṃ dvārasaṃgrahec tam uvāca muniṃ vākyaṃ kathayasveti rāghavaḥa yat te manīṣitaṃ vākyaṃ yena vāsi samāhitaḥc kathayasva viśaṅkas tvaṃ mamāpi hṛdi vartatea śṛṇu rāma mahābāho yadartham aham āhataḥc pitāmahena devena preṣito smi mahābalaa tavāhaṃ pūrvake bhāve putraḥ parapuraṃjayac māyāsaṃbhāvito vīra kālaḥ sarvasamāharaḥa pitāmahaś ca bhagavān āha lokapatiḥ prabhuḥc samayas te mahābāho svarlokān parirakṣituma saṃkṣipya ca purā lokān māyayā svayam eva hic mahārṇave śayāno psu māṃ tvaṃ pūrvam ajījanaḥa bhogavantaṃ tato nāgam anantam udake śayamc māyayā janayitvā tvaṃ dvau ca sattvau mahābalaua madhuṃ ca kaiṭabhaṃ caiva yayor asthicayair vṛtāc iyaṃ parvatasaṃbādhā medinī cābhavan mahīa padme divyārkasaṃkāśe nābhyām utpādya mām apic prājāpatyaṃ tvayā karma sarvaṃ mayi niveśitama so haṃ saṃnyastabhāro hi tvām upāse jagatpatimc rakṣāṃ vidhatsva bhūteṣu mama tejaḥ karo bhavāna tatas tvam api durdharṣas tasmād bhāvāt sanātanātc rakṣārthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viṣṇutvam upajagmivāna adityāṃ vīryavān putro bhrātṝṇāṃ harṣavardhanaḥc samutpanneṣu kṛtyeṣu lokasāhyāya kalpasea sa tvaṃ vitrāsyamānāsu prajāsu jagatāṃ varac rāvaṇasya vadhākāṅkṣī mānuṣeṣu mano dadhāḥa daśavarṣasahasrāṇi daśavarṣaśatāni cac kṛtvā vāsasya niyatiṃ svayam evātmanaḥ purāa sa tvaṃ manomayaḥ putraḥ pūrṇāyur mānuṣeṣv ihac kālo naravaraśreṣṭha samīpam upavartituma yadi bhūyo mahārāja prajā icchasy upāsitumc vasa vā vīra bhadraṃ te evam āha pitāmahaḥa atha vā vijigīṣā te suralokāya rāghavac sanāthā viṣṇunā devā bhavantu vigatajvarāḥa śrutvā pitāmahenoktaṃ vākyaṃ kālasamīritamc rāghavaḥ prahasan vākyaṃ sarvasaṃhāram abravīta śrutaṃ me devadevasya vākyaṃ paramam adbhutamc prītir hi mahatī jātā tavāgamanasaṃbhavāa bhadraṃ te stu gamiṣyāmi yata evāham āgataḥc hṛd gato hy asi saṃprāpto na me sty atra vicāraṇāa mayā hi sarvakṛtyeṣu devānāṃ vaśavartināmc sthātavyaṃ sarvasaṃhāre yathā hy āha pitāmahaḥa tathā tayoḥ kathayator durvāsā bhagavān ṛṣiḥc rāmasya darśanākāṅkṣī rājadvāram upāgamata so bhigamya ca saumitrim uvāca ṛṣisattamaḥc rāmaṃ darśaya me śīghraṃ purā me rtho tivartatea munes tu bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahāc abhivādya mahātmānaṃ vākyam etad uvāca haa kiṃ kāryaṃ brūhi bhagavan ko vārthaḥ kiṃ karomy ahamc vyagro hi rāghavo brahman muhūrtaṃ vā pratīkṣatāma tac chrutvā ṛṣiśārdūlaḥ krodhena kaluṣīkṛtaḥc uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ nirdahann iva cakṣuṣāa asmin kṣaṇe māṃ saumitre rāmāya prativedayac viṣayaṃ tvāṃ puraṃ caiva śapiṣye rāghavaṃ tathāa bharataṃ caiva saumitre yuṣmākaṃ yā ca saṃtatiḥc na hi śakṣyāmy ahaṃ bhūyo manyuṃ dhārayituṃ hṛdia tac chrutvā ghorasaṃkāśaṃ vākyaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥc cintayām āsa manasā tasya vākyasya niścayama ekasya maraṇaṃ me stu mā bhūt sarvavināśanamc iti buddhyā viniścitya rāghavāya nyavedayata lakṣmaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaḥ kālaṃ visṛjya cac niṣpatya tvaritaṃ rājā atreḥ putraṃ dadarśa haa so bhivādya mahātmānaṃ jvalantam iva tejasāc kiṃ kāryam iti kākutsthaḥ kṛtāñjalir abhāṣataa tad vākyaṃ rāghaveṇṇoktaṃ śrutvā munivaraḥ prabhuḥc pratyāha rāmaṃ durvāsāḥ śrūyatāṃ dharmavatsalaa adya varṣasahasrasya samāptir mama rāghavac so haṃ bhojanam icchāmi yathāsiddhaṃ tavānaghaa tac chrutvā vacanaṃ rāmo harṣeṇa mahatānvitaḥc bhojanaṃ munimukhyāya yathāsiddham upāharata sa tu bhuktvā muniśreṣṭhas tad annam amṛtopamamc sādhu rāmeti saṃbhāṣya svam āśramam upāgamata tasmin gate mahātejā rāghavaḥ prītamānasaḥc saṃsmṛtya kālavākyāni tato duḥkham upeyivāna duḥkhena ca susaṃtaptaḥ smṛtvā tad ghoradarśanamc avānmukho dīnamanā vyāhartuṃ na śaśāka haa tato buddhyā viniścitya kālavākyāni rāghavaḥc naitad astīti coktvā sa tūṣṇīm āsīn mahāyaśāḥa avāṅmukham atho dīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā somam ivāplutamc rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇo vākyaṃ hṛṣṭo madhuram abravīta na saṃtāpaṃ mahābāho madarthaṃ kartum arhasic pūrvanirmāṇabaddhā hi kālasya gatir īdṛśīa jahi māṃ saumya visrabdaḥ pratijñāṃ paripālayac hīnapratijñāḥ kākutstha prayānti narakaṃ narāḥa yadi prītir mahārāja yady anugrāhyatā mayic jahi māṃ nirviśaṅkas tvaṃ dharmaṃ vardhaya rāghavaa lakṣmaṇena tathoktas tu rāmaḥ pracalitendriyaḥc mantriṇaḥ samupānīya tathaiva ca purodhasaṃa abravīc ca yathāvṛttaṃ teṣāṃ madhye narādhipaḥc durvāsobhigamaṃ caiva pratijñāṃ tāpasasya caa tac chrutvā mantriṇaḥ sarve sopādhyāyāḥ samāsatac vasiṣṭhas tu mahātejā vākyam etad uvāca haa dṛṣṭam etan mahābāho kṣayaṃ te lomaharṣaṇamc lakṣmaṇena viyogaś ca tava rāma mahāyaśaḥa tyajainaṃ balavān kālo mā pratijñāṃ vṛthā kṛthāḥc vinaṣṭāyāṃ pratijñāyāṃ dharmo hi vilayaṃ vrajeta tato dharme vinaṣṭe tu trailokye sacarācaramc sadevarṣigaṇaṃ sarvaṃ vinaśyeta na saṃśayaḥa sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla trailokyasyābhipālanamc lakṣmaṇasya vadhenādya jagat svasthaṃ kuruṣva haa teṣāṃ tat samavetānāṃ vākyaṃ dharmārthasaṃhitamc śrutvā pariṣado madhye rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīta visarjaye tvāṃ saumitre mā bhūd dharmaviparyayaḥc tyāgo vadho vā vihitaḥ sādhūnām ubhayaṃ samama rāmeṇa bhāṣite vākye bāṣpavyākulitekṣaṇaḥc lakṣmaṇas tvaritaḥ prāyāt svagṛhaṃ na viveśa haa sa gatvā sarayūtīram upaspṛśya kṛtāñjaliḥc nigṛhya sarvasrotāṃsi niḥśvāsaṃ na mumoca haa anucchvasantaṃ yuktaṃ taṃ saśakrāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥc devāḥ sarṣigaṇāḥ sarve puṣpair avakiraṃs tadāa adṛśyaṃ sarvam anujaiḥ saśarīraṃ mahābalamc pragṛhya lakṣmaṇaṃ śakro divaṃ saṃpraviveśa haa tato viṣṇoś caturbhāgam āgataṃ surasattamāḥc hṛṣṭāḥ pramuditāḥ sarve pūjayan ṛṣibhiḥ sahaa visṛjya lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥc purodhasaṃ mantriṇaś ca naigamāṃś cedam abravīta adya rājye bhiṣekṣyāmi bharataṃ dharmavatsalamc ayodhyāyāṃ patiṃ vīraṃ tato yāsyāmy ahaṃ vanama praveśayata saṃbhārān mā bhūt kālātyayo yathāc adyaivāhaṃ gamiṣyāmi lakṣmaṇena gatāṃ gatima tac chrutvā rāghaveṇoktaṃ sarvāḥ prakṛtayo bhṛśamc mūrdhabhiḥ praṇatā bhūmau gatasattvā ivābhavana bharataś ca visaṃjño bhūc chrutvā rāmasya bhāṣitamc rājyaṃ vigarhayām āsa rāghavaṃ cedam abravīta satyena hi śape rājan svargaloke na caiva hic na kāmaye yathā rājyaṃ tvāṃ vinā raghunandanaa imau kuśīlavau rājann abhiṣiñca narādhipac kosaleṣu kuśaṃ vīram uttareṣu tathā lavama śatrughnasya tu gacchantu dūtās tvaritavikramāḥc idaṃ gamanam asmākaṃ svargāyākhyāntu mācirama tac chrutvā bharatenoktaṃ dṛṣṭvā cāpi hy adho mukhānc paurān duḥkhena saṃtaptān vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīta vatsa rāma imāḥ paśya dharaṇīṃ prakṛtīr gatāḥc jñātvaiṣām īpsitaṃ kāryaṃ mā caiṣāṃ vipriyaṃ kṛthāḥa vasiṣṭhasya tu vākyena utthāpya prakṛtījanamc kiṃ karomīti kākutsthaḥ sarvān vacanam abravīta tataḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayo rāmaṃ vacanam abruvanc gacchantam anugacchāmo yato rāma gamiṣyasia eṣā naḥ paramā prītir eṣa dharmaḥ paro mataḥc hṛdgatā naḥ sadā tuṣṭis tavānugamane dṛḍhāa paureṣu yadi te prītir yadi sneho hy anuttamaḥc saputradārāḥ kākutstha samaṃ gacchāma satpathama tapovanaṃ vā durgaṃ vā nadīm ambhonidhiṃ tathāc vayaṃ te yadi na tyājyāḥ sarvān no naya īśvaraa sa teṣāṃ niścayaṃ jñātvā kṛtāntaṃ ca nirīkṣyacac paurāṇāṃ dṛḍhabhaktiṃ ca bāḍham ity eva so bravīta evaṃ viniścayaṃ kṛtvā tasminn ahani rāghavaḥc kosaleṣu kuśaṃ vīram uttareṣu tathā lavama abhiṣiñcan mahātmānāv ubhāv eva kuśīlavauc rathānāṃ tu sahasrāṇi trīṇi nāgāyutāni caa daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi ekaikasya dhanaṃ dadauc bahuratnau bahudhanau hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtaua abhiṣicya tu tau vīrau prasthāpya svapure tathāc dūtān saṃpreṣayām āsa śatrughnāya mahātmanea te dūtā rāmavākyena coditā laghuvikramāḥc prajagmur madhurāṃ śīghraṃ cakrur vāsaṃ na cādhvania tatas tribhir aho rātraiḥ saṃprāpya madhurām athac śatrughnāya yathāvṛttam ācakhyuḥ sarvam eva tata lakṣmaṇasya parityāgaṃ pratijñāṃ rāghavasya cac putrayor abhiṣekaṃ ca paurānugamanaṃ tathāa kuśasya nagarī ramyā vindhyaparvatarodhasic kuśāvatīti nāmnā sā kṛtā rāmeṇa dhīmatāa śrāvitā ca purī ramyā śrāvatīti lavasya cac ayodhyāṃ vijanāṃ caiva bharataṃ rāghavānugama evaṃ sarvaṃ nivedyāśu śatrughnāya mahātmanec viremus te tato dūtās tvara rājann iti bruvana śrutvā taṃ ghorasaṃkāśaṃ kulakṣayam upasthitamc prakṛtīs tu samānīya kāñcanaṃ ca purohitama teṣāṃ sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam ākhyāya raghunandanaḥc ātmanaś ca viparyāsaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahaa tataḥ putradvayaṃ vīraḥ so bhyaṣiñcan narādhipaḥc subāhur madhurāṃ lebhe śatrughātī ca vaidiśama dvidhākṛtvā tu tāṃ senāṃ mādhurīṃ putrayor dvayoḥc dhanadhānyasamāyuktau sthāpayām āsa pārthivaua tato visṛjya rājānaṃ vaidiśe śatrughātinamc jagāma tvarito yodhyāṃ rathenaikena rāghavaḥa sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakamc kṣaumasūkṣmāmbaradharaṃ munibhiḥ sārdham akṣayaiḥa so bhivādya tato rāmaṃ prāñjaliḥ prayatendriyaḥc uvāca vākyaṃ dharmajño dharmam evānucintayana kṛtvābhiṣekaṃ sutayor yuktaṃ rāghavayor dhanaiḥc tavānugamane rājan viddhi māṃ kṛtaniścayama na cānyad atra vaktavyaṃ dustaraṃ tava śāsanamc tyaktuṃ nārhasi māṃ vīra bhaktimantaṃ viśeṣataḥa tasya tāṃ buddhim aklībāṃ vijñāya raghunandanaḥc bāḍham ity eva śatrughnaṃ rāmo vacanam abravīta tasya vākyasya vākyānte vānarāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥc ṛkṣarākṣasasaṃghāś ca samāpetur anekaśaḥa devaputrā ṛṣisutā gandharvāṇāṃ sutās tathāc rāma kṣayaṃ viditvā te sarva eva samāgatāḥa te rāmam abhivādyāhuḥ sarva eva samāgatāḥc tavānugamane rājan saṃprāptāḥ sma mahāyaśaḥa yadi rāma vināsmābhir gacches tvaṃ puruṣarṣabhac yamadaṇḍam ivodyamya tvayā sma vinipātitāḥa evaṃ teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā ṛṣkavānararakṣasāmc vibhīṣaṇam athovāca madhuraṃ ślakṣṇayā girāa yāvat prajā dhariṣyanti tāvat tvaṃ vai vibhīṣaṇac rākṣasendra mahāvīrya laṅkāsthaḥ svaṃ dhariṣyasia prajāḥ saṃrakṣa dharmeṇa nottaraṃ vaktum arhasia tam evam uktvā kākutstho hanūmantam athābravītc jīvite kṛtabuddhis tvaṃ mā pratijñāṃ vilopayaa matkathāḥ pracariṣyanti yāval loke harīśvarac tāvat tvaṃ dhārayan prāṇān pratijñām anupālayaa tathaivam uktvā kākutsthaḥ sarvāṃs tān ṛkṣavānarānc mayā sārdhaṃ prayāteti tadā tān rāghavo bravīta prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ pṛthuvakṣā mahāyaśāḥc rāmaḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥ purodhasam athābravīta agnihotraṃ vrajatv agre sarpir jvalitapāvakamc vājapeyātapatraṃ ca śobhayānaṃ mahāpathama tato vasiṣṭhas tejasvī sarvaṃ niravaśeṣataḥc cakāra vidhivad dharmyaṃ mahāprāsthānikaṃ vidhima tataḥ kṣaumāmbaradharo brahma cāvartayan paramc kuśān gṛhītvā pāṇibhyāṃ prasajya prayayāv athaa avyāharan kva cit kiṃ cin niśceṣṭo niḥsukhaḥ pathic nirjagāma gṛhāt tasmād dīpyamāno yathāṃśumāna rāmasya pārśve savye tu padmā śrīḥ susamāhitāc dakṣiṇe hrīr viśālākṣī vyavasāyas tathāgrataḥa śarā nānāvidhāś cāpi dhanur āyatavigrahamc anuvrajanti kākutsthaṃ sarve puruṣavigrahāḥa vedā brāhmaṇarūpeṇa sāvitrī sarvarakṣiṇīc oṃkāro tha vaṣaṭkāraḥ sarve rāmam anuvratāḥa ṛṣayaś ca mahātmānaḥ sarva eva mahīsurāḥc anvagacchanta kākutsthaṃ svargadvāram upāgatama taṃ yāntam anuyānti sma antaḥpuracarāḥ striyaḥc savṛddhabāladāsīkāḥ savarṣavarakiṃkarāḥa sāntaḥpuraś ca bharataḥ śatrughnasahito yayauc rāmavratam upāgamya rāghavaṃ samanuvratāḥa tato viprā mahātmānaḥ sāgnihotrāḥ samāhitāḥc saputradārāḥ kākutstham anvagacchan mahāmatima mantriṇo bhṛtyavargāś ca saputrāḥ sahabāndhavāḥc sānugā rāghavaṃ sarve anvagacchan prahṛṣṭavata tataḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayo hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtāḥc anujagmuḥ pragacchantaṃ rāghavaṃ guṇarañjitāḥa snātaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ hṛṣṭapuṣpam anuttamamc dṛptaṃ kilikilāśabdaiḥ sarvaṃ rāmam anuvratama na tatra kaś cid dīno bhūd vrīḍito vāpi duḥkhitaḥc hṛṣṭaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ babhūva paramādbhutama draṣṭukāmo tha niryāṇaṃ rājño jānapado janaḥc saṃprāptaḥ so pi dṛṣṭvaiva saha sarvair anuvrataḥa ṛkṣavānararakṣāṃsi janāś ca puravāsinaḥc agachan parayā bhaktyā pṛṣṭhataḥ susamāhitāḥa adhyardhayojanaṃ gatvā nadīṃ paścān mukhāśritāmc sarayūṃ puṇyasalilāṃ dadarśa raghunandanaḥa atha tasmin muhūrte tu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥc sarvaiḥ parivṛto devair ṛṣibhiś ca mahātmabhiḥa āyayau yatra kākutsthaḥ svargāya samupasthitaḥc vimānaśatakoṭībhir divyābhir abhisaṃvṛtaḥa papāta puṣpavṛṣṭiś ca vāyumuktā mahaughavata tasmiṃs tūryaśatākīrṇe gandharvāpsarasaṃkulec sarayūsalilaṃ rāmaḥ padbhyāṃ samupacakramea tataḥ pitāmaho vāṇīm antarikṣād abhāṣatac āgaccha viṣṇo bhadraṃ te diṣṭyā prāpto si rāghavaa bhrātṛbhiḥ saha devābhaiḥ praviśasva svakāṃ tanumc vaiṣṇavīṃ tāṃ mahātejas tad ākāśaṃ sanātanama tvaṃ hi lokagatir deva na tvāṃ ke cit prajānatec ṛte māyāṃ viśālākṣa tava pūrvaparigrahāma tvam acintyaṃ mahad bhūtam akṣayaṃ sarvasaṃgrahamc yām icchasi mahātejas tāṃ tanuṃ praviśa svayama pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā viniścitya mahāmatiḥc viveśa vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaḥ saśarīraḥ sahānujaḥa tato viṣṇugataṃ devaṃ pūjayanti sma devatāḥc sādhyā marudgaṇāś caiva sendrāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥa ye ca divyā ṛṣigaṇā gandharvāpsarasaś ca yāḥc suparṇanāgayakṣāś ca daityadānavarākṣasāḥa sarvaṃ hṛṣṭaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ pūrṇamanorathamc sādhu sādhv iti tat sarvaṃ tridivaṃ gatakalmaṣama atha viṣṇur mahātejāḥ pitāmaham uvāca hac eṣāṃ lokāñ janaughānāṃ dātum arhasi suvrataa ime hi sarve snehān mām anuyātā manasvinaḥc bhaktā bhājayitavyāś ca tyaktātmānaś ca matkṛtea tac chrutvā viṣṇuvacanaṃ brahmā lokaguruḥ prabhuḥc lokān sāntānikān nāma yāsyantīme samāgatāḥa yac ca tiryaggataṃ kiṃ cid rāmam evānucintayatc prāṇāṃs tyakṣyati bhaktyā vai saṃtāne tu nivatsyatie sarvair eva guṇair yukte brahmalokād anantarea vānarāś ca svakāṃ yonim ṛkṣāś caiva tathā yayuḥc yebhyo viniḥsṛtā ye ye surādibhyaḥ susaṃbhavāḥa ṛṣibhyo nāgayakṣebhyas tāṃs tān eva prapedirec tathoktavati deveśe gopratāram upāgatāḥa bhejire sarayūṃ sarve harṣapūrṇāśruviklavāḥc avagāhya jalaṃ yo yaḥ prāṇī hy āsīt prahṛṣṭavata mānuṣaṃ deham utsṛjya vimānaṃ so dhyarohatac tiryagyonigatāś cāpi saṃprāptāḥ sarayūjalama divyā divyena vapuṣā devā dīptā ivābhavanc gatvā tu sarayūtoyaṃ sthāvarāṇi carāṇi caa prāpya tat toyavikledaṃ devalokam upāgamanc devānāṃ yasya yā yonir vānarā ṛṣka rākṣasāḥa tām eva viviśuḥ sarve devān nikṣipya cāmbhasic tathā svargagataṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā lokagurur divama jagāma tridaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ hṛṣṭair hṛṣṭo mahāmatiḥ
